    70   // Auth state listener — reads role from custom claims first, Firestore as fallback
    71   useEffect(() => {
    72     const unsubscribe = onAuthStateChanged(auth, async (currentUser) => {
    73       if (currentUser) {
    74         setUser(currentUser);
    75         try {
    76           // 1. Try custom claims first (most secure, included in ID token)
    77           const idTokenResult = await currentUser.getIdTokenResult(true);
    78           const claimRole = idTokenResult.claims.role as string | undefined;
    79 
    80           if (claimRole) {
    81             const normalized = normalizeRole(claimRole);
    82             setRole(normalized);
    83             if (normalized) {
    84               cacheUserProfile(currentUser.uid, currentUser.email || '', normalized, currentUser.displayName || undefined);
    85               invalidateStaleCache(normalized, getDepartment(normalized));
    86             }
    87           } else {
    88             // 2. Fallback to Firestore users/{uid} document
    89             const snap = await getDoc(doc(db, 'users', currentUser.uid));
    90             const roleValue = snap.exists() ? normalizeRole(snap.data().role as string) : null;
    91             setRole(roleValue);
    92             if (roleValue) {
    93               cacheUserProfile(currentUser.uid, currentUser.email || '', roleValue, currentUser.displayName || undefined);
    94               invalidateStaleCache(roleValue, getDepartment(roleValue));
    95             }
    96           }
    97         } catch {
    98           // If both claims and Firestore fail, try cached role
    99           const cached = getCachedUserProfile();
   100           if (cached && cached.uid === currentUser.uid) {
   101             const normalized = normalizeRole(cached.role);
   102             setRole(normalized);
   103             if (normalized) {
   104               invalidateStaleCache(normalized, getDepartment(normalized));
   105             }
   106           } else {
   107             setRole(null);
   108           }
   109         }
   110       } else {
   111         setUser(null);
   112         setRole(null);
   113       }
   114       setLoading(false);
   115     });

```
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { createUserWithEmailAndPassword } from 'firebase/auth';
import { auth } from '@/lib/firebase';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';
import { Building2, Eye, EyeOff } from 'lucide-react';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

export default function Register() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');
  const [confirmPassword, setConfirmPassword] = useState('');
  const [showPassword, setShowPassword] = useState(false);
  const [showConfirm, setShowConfirm] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState('');
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setError('');

    if (!email.trim() || !password.trim() || !confirmPassword.trim()) {
      setError('အီးမေးလ်၊ စကားဝှက် နှင့် အတည်ပြုစကားဝှက် အားလုံး ဖြည့်ရန်လိုအပ်ပါသည်။');
      return;
    }

    if (password !== confirmPassword) {
      setError('စကားဝှက်နှင့် အတည်ပြုစကားဝှက် ကိုက်ညီမှု မရှိပါ။');
      return;
    }

    if (password.length < 6) {
      setError('စကားဝှက် အနည်းဆုံး ၆ လုံးဖြစ်ရန်လိုအပ်ပါသည်။');
      return;
    }

    setLoading(true);
    try {
      await createUserWithEmailAndPassword(auth, email.trim(), password);
      toast.success('အကောင့်ဖွင့်ခြင်း အောင်မြင်ပါသည်');
      navigate('/dashboard');
    } catch (err: any) {
      const msg = err?.message || '';
      if (msg.includes('email-already-in-use')) {
        setError('ဤအီးမေးလ်ဖြင့် အကောင့်ရှိပြီးသားဖြစ်ပါသည်။');
      } else if (msg.includes('invalid-email')) {
        setError('အီးမေးလ် ပုံစံ မမှန်ကန်ပါ။');
      } else if (msg.includes('weak-password')) {
        setError('စကားဝှက် အားနည်းနေပါသည်။ အနည်းဆုံး ၆ လုံး ထည့်သွင်းပါ။');
      } else {
        setError('အကောင့်ဖွင့်ရာတွင် အမှားဖြစ်သွားပါသည်။ ပြန်လည်ကြိုးစားပါ။');
      }
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-[#F8FAFC] px-4">
      <div className="w-full max-w-md animate-fade-in-up space-y-3">
        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-card p-8">
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center mb-8">
            <div className="w-14 h-14 rounded-xl gradient-primary flex items-center justify-center mb-4 shadow-card">
              <Building2 className="w-7 h-7 text-white" />
            </div>
            <h1 className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground">Create Account</h1>
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-1">PSM Sale CRM အကောင့်အသစ်ဖွင့်ရန်</p>
          </div>

          <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-5">
            <div className="space-y-2">
              <Label htmlFor="reg-email" className="text-sm font-medium">အီးမေးလ်</Label>
              <Input
                id="reg-email"
                type="email"
                placeholder="you@company.com"
                value={email}
                onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
                required
                className="h-12"
              />
            </div>

            <div className="space-y-2">
              <Label htmlFor="reg-password" className="text-sm font-medium">စကားဝှက်</Label>
              <div className="relative">
                <Input
                  id="reg-password"
                  type={showPassword ? 'text' : 'password'}
                  placeholder="အနည်းဆုံး ၆ လုံး"
                  value={password}
                  onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}
                  required
                  minLength={6}
                  className="h-12 pr-12"
                />
                <button
                  type="button"
                  onClick={() => setShowPassword(!showPassword)}
                  className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-9 h-9 flex items-center justify-center rounded-full text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground hover:bg-muted active:bg-muted/80 transition-colors"
                >
                  {showPassword ? <EyeOff className="w-4 h-4" /> : <Eye className="w-4 h-4" />}
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="space-y-2">
              <Label htmlFor="reg-confirm" className="text-sm font-medium">အတည်ပြုစကားဝှက်</Label>
              <div className="relative">
                <Input
                  id="reg-confirm"
                  type={showConfirm ? 'text' : 'password'}
                  placeholder="စကားဝှက်ထပ်မံ ထည့်သွင်းပါ"
                  value={confirmPassword}
                  onChange={(e) => setConfirmPassword(e.target.value)}
                  required
                  minLength={6}
                  className="h-12 pr-12"
                />
                <button
                  type="button"
                  onClick={() => setShowConfirm(!showConfirm)}
                  className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-9 h-9 flex items-center justify-center rounded-full text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground hover:bg-muted active:bg-muted/80 transition-colors"
                >
                  {showConfirm ? <EyeOff className="w-4 h-4" /> : <Eye className="w-4 h-4" />}
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>

            {error && (
              <div className="text-sm text-destructive bg-destructive/10 rounded-md px-3 py-2">
                {error}
              </div>
            )}

            <Button
              type="submit"
              disabled={loading}
              className="w-full h-12 gradient-primary hover:gradient-primary-hover text-white font-medium transition-all duration-300 hover:shadow-card-hover active:scale-[0.98]"
            >
              {loading ? 'ဖွင့်နေသည်...' : 'အကောင့်ဖွင့်ရန်'}
            </Button>

            <div className="text-center">
              <button
                type="button"
                onClick={() => navigate('/login')}
                className="text-sm text-primary hover:underline"
              >
                ရှိပြီးသား အကောင့်ဖြင့် ဝင်ရောက်ရန်
              </button>
            </div>
          </form>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function exportAsHTML(leads: Lead[]) {
```
New String: ```
export function exportAsCSV(leads: Lead[]) {
  if (leads.length === 0) return;
  const headers = ['Name', 'Phone', 'Project', 'Status'];
  const rows = leads.map((l) => [
    l.name,
    l.phone,
    l.preferredProject || '',
    l.status,
  ]);
  const csvContent = [headers, ...rows]
    .map((row) =>
      row.map((cell) => {
        const val = String(cell ?? '');
        if (val.includes(',') || val.includes('"') || val.includes('\n')) {
          return `"${val.replace(/"/g, '""')}"`;
        }
        return val;
      }).join(',')
    )
    .join('\n');
  const blob = new Blob(['\uFEFF' + csvContent], { type: 'text/csv;charset=utf-8;' });
  triggerDownload(blob, `PSM_Leads_${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.csv`);
}

export function exportAsHTML(leads: Lead[]) {
```

    15 export function useStatusColors() {
    16   const [colors, setColors] = useState<Record<string, string>>(DEFAULT_COLORS);
    17   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    18 
    19   useEffect(() => {
    20     const loadColors = async () => {
    21       try {
    22         const snap = await getDoc(doc(db, 'settings', 'chartColors'));
    23         if (snap.exists()) {
    24           const data = snap.data() as Record<string, string>;
    25           const merged: Record<string, string> = {};
    26           for (const s of STATUSES) {
    27             merged[s] = data[s] || DEFAULT_COLORS[s];
    28           }
    29           setColors(merged);
    30         }
    31       } catch {
    32         // Fallback to defaults on error
    33       } finally {
    34         setLoading(false);
    35       }
    36     };
    37     loadColors();

    27 export default function StatusColorDialog({ colors, onSave }: StatusColorDialogProps) {

SkillObservation(content='Base directory for this skill: /workspace/app-chfyozakqsqp/.skills/large-language-model\n\n# Large Language Model (Gemini 2.5 Flash)\n\n## Capability Overview\n\nCall the Gemini 2.5 Flash multimodal large language model via the API Gateway. Supports text conversation and image understanding, with responses returned as an SSE stream.\n\n- **Endpoint**: `POST https://app-chfyozakqsqp-api-VaOwP8E7dJqa.gateway.appmedo.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash:streamGenerateContent?alt=sse`\n- **Response mode**: SSE streaming (Server-Sent Events)\n- **Supported modalities**: Multi-turn text conversation, Base64 inline images, file URI images\n- **First-token latency**: Up to 30 seconds; extend API timeout settings accordingly\n- **Billing**: Standard price ¥0.30 / call, discounted price ¥0.19 / call\n\n### Request Body Structure (Overview)\n\n| Field | Type | Required | Description |\n|-------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `contents` | array | Yes | Array of conversation turns, each containing `role` and `parts` |\n| `contents[].role` | string | Yes | `"user"` or `"model"` |\n| `contents[].parts` | array | Yes | Message parts; each part contains one of `text`, `inlineData`, or `fileData` |\n\n### Response Structure (SSE stream, per-frame example)\n\n```json\n{\n  "candidates": [\n    {\n      "content": {\n        "role": "model",\n        "parts": [{ "text": "That\'s easy! Each dog has 4 paws..." }]\n      },\n      "finishReason": "STOP",\n      "index": 0,\n      "safetyRatings": []\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n> Read `references/stream-generate-api.md` for the full parameter table, response field descriptions, and complete code for both generation-time and post-generation usage.\n\n---\n\n## End-to-End Workflow\n\n1. The client sends the conversation history (`contents` array) to the Edge Function.\n2. The Edge Function reads `INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY` from the Deno environment, attaches the `X-Gateway-Authorization` header, and calls the upstream endpoint via POST.\n3. The upstream responds with an SSE stream; the Edge Function **passes the stream through directly** without buffering.\n4. The frontend consumes the stream with `ky` + `eventsource-parser` and renders Markdown with `streamdown`.\n\n---\n\n## Generation-Time Usage (Agent Direct Call)\n\nSee `references/stream-generate-api.md` — **Generation-Time Usage** section.\n\nKey points: Call the gateway directly via `fetch`, inject the platform key with `X-Gateway-Authorization: Bearer ${apiKey}`, and read the SSE stream line-by-line, parsing each frame\'s JSON.\n\n---\n\n## Post-Generation Usage (In-App via Edge Function)\n\nSee `references/stream-generate-api.md` — **Post-Generation Usage** section.\n\nKey points: The Edge Function passes through the upstream SSE stream; the frontend depends on `ky@^1.2.3`, `eventsource-parser@^3.0.3`, and optionally `streamdown@^1.1.6` for Markdown rendering.\n\n---\n\n## Notes\n\n- **Key security**: `INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY` may only be read server-side in the Edge Function; never expose it to the frontend.\n- **Timeout**: First token can take up to 30 seconds; extend the frontend request timeout accordingly (recommend ≥ 60s).\n- **Error handling**: Always handle 429 (quota exceeded) and 402 (insufficient balance) and display friendly messages to the user.\n- **Billing**: Each call costs ¥0.19 (discounted); avoid unnecessary repeated calls (e.g., rapid successive clicks by the user).\n- **Streaming dependency**: The frontend must use `EventSource` or `eventsource-parser` to consume SSE; do not use a plain `fetch().json()`.\n- **Markdown rendering**: Model responses contain Markdown formatting; it is recommended to use `streamdown@^1.1.6` for real-time rendering.', observation=<ObservationType.SKILL: 'skill'>, skill='large-language-model', success=True, data={'skill_path': '/workspace/miaoda_skills/prompts/managed/large-language-model/SKILL.md', 'scripts_path': None})

     9 - **Method**: POST

    12 - **Response**: SSE stream (text/event-stream)

    17 
    18 ### Top-Level Fields
    19 
    20 | Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
    21 |-----------|------|----------|-------------|
    22 | `contents` | array | Yes | Array of conversation turns, ordered sequentially |
    23 
    24 ### `contents[]` Object
    25 
    26 | Field | Type | Required | Description |
    27 |-------|------|----------|-------------|
    28 | `role` | string | Yes | Message sender; value is `"user"` or `"model"` |
    29 | `parts` | array | Yes | Array of message parts; each part contains one of the three options below |
    30 
    31 ### `parts[]` Part (one of three)
    32 
    33 | Field | Type | Required | Description |
    34 |-------|------|----------|-------------|
    35 | `text` | string | Conditionally required | Plain text input |
    36 | `inlineData` | object | Conditionally required | Inline media (Base64) |
    37 | `inlineData.mimeType` | string | Required (when using inlineData) | MIME type, e.g. `image/jpeg`, `image/png` |
    38 | `inlineData.data` | string | Required (when using inlineData) | Base64-encoded media data |
    39 | `fileData` | object | Conditionally required | URI media data |
    40 | `fileData.mimeType` | string | Required (when using fileData) | MIME type |
    41 | `fileData.fileUri` | string | Required (when using fileData) | File URI |
    42

    44 
    45 ## Response Fields
    46 
    47 Each SSE frame contains a JSON object:
    48 
    49 | Field Path | Type | Description |
    50 |------------|------|-------------|
    51 | `candidates` | array | List of candidate responses generated by the model |
    52 | `candidates[].content` | object | Message content returned by the model |
    53 | `candidates[].content.role` | string | Always `"model"` |
    54 | `candidates[].content.parts` | array | Array of response parts |
    55 | `candidates[].content.parts[].text` | string | Text chunk generated by the model |
    56 | `candidates[].finishReason` | string? | Stop reason: `STOP` (normal) / `MAX_TOKENS` (limit exceeded) / `SAFETY` (safety filter) |
    57 | `candidates[].index` | number | Candidate index, typically 0 |
    58 | `candidates[].safetyRatings` | array | Safety rating list (may be an empty array) |
    59 
    60 > In streaming mode, `finishReason` only appears in the final frame (with a value such as `"STOP"`); intermediate frames typically have `null` or the field is absent.

```
import { serve } from 'https://deno.land/std@0.192.0/http/server.ts';

const API_ENDPOINT = 'https://app-chfyozakqsqp-api-VaOwP8E7dJqa.gateway.appmedo.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash:streamGenerateContent?alt=sse';

interface LeadData {
  name?: string;
  phone?: string;
  email?: string;
  interestType?: string;
  propertyType?: string;
  preferredProject?: string;
  budgetRange?: string;
  purpose?: string;
  urgency?: string;
  paymentMethod?: string;
  leadSource?: string;
  currentLocation?: string;
  remarks?: string;
}

function buildPrompt(lead: LeadData): string {
  return `You are a real estate CRM AI scoring assistant. Analyze the following lead data and score it as A, B, or C based on buying intent, budget clarity, urgency, and source quality.

Scoring criteria:
- A (Hot/Ready): Clear budget, urgent timeline, high-quality source, specific project interest, ready to view/buy
- B (Warm/Considering): Moderate budget range, some urgency, considering options, needs follow-up
- C (Cold/Inquiring): Vague budget, no urgency, just browsing, low-quality source

Lead data:
${JSON.stringify(lead, null, 2)}

Respond ONLY in this exact JSON format (no markdown, no extra text):
{"score":"A|B|C","reasoning":"brief reason in Myanmar language"}`;
}

async function callGemini(prompt: string, apiKey: string): Promise<{ score: string; reasoning: string }> {
  const body = {
    contents: [
      {
        role: 'user',
        parts: [{ text: prompt }],
      },
    ],
  };

  const response = await fetch(API_ENDPOINT, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      'X-Gateway-Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
    },
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
  });

  if (!response.ok) {
    const text = await response.text().catch(() => '');
    throw new Error(`Gemini API error ${response.status}: ${text}`);
  }

  const reader = response.body?.getReader();
  if (!reader) throw new Error('No response body');

  const decoder = new TextDecoder();
  let fullText = '';

  while (true) {
    const { done, value } = await reader.read();
    if (done) break;
    const chunk = decoder.decode(value, { stream: true });
    for (const line of chunk.split('\n')) {
      const trimmed = line.trim();
      if (!trimmed.startsWith('data:')) continue;
      const dataStr = trimmed.slice(5).trim();
      if (!dataStr || dataStr === '[DONE]') continue;
      try {
        const parsed = JSON.parse(dataStr);
        const text = parsed.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text;
        if (text) fullText += text;
      } catch {
        // skip malformed lines
      }
    }
  }

  // Extract JSON from response
  const jsonMatch = fullText.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/);
  if (!jsonMatch) {
    throw new Error('Could not parse AI response: ' + fullText.slice(0, 200));
  }

  const result = JSON.parse(jsonMatch[0]);
  return {
    score: String(result.score || 'C').trim().toUpperCase(),
    reasoning: String(result.reasoning || 'No reasoning provided.'),
  };
}

serve(async (req) => {
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') {
    return new Response(null, {
      status: 204,
      headers: {
        'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'POST, OPTIONS',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type, Authorization',
      },
    });
  }

  try {
    const apiKey = Deno.env.get('INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY');
    if (!apiKey) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ error: 'Server configuration error' }),
        { status: 500, headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' } }
      );
    }

    const { lead } = await req.json();
    if (!lead) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ error: 'Missing lead data' }),
        { status: 400, headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' } }
      );
    }

    const prompt = buildPrompt(lead);
    const result = await callGemini(prompt, apiKey);

    // Map to full level string
    const levelMap: Record<string, string> = {
      'A': 'Level A (Hot/Ready)',
      'B': 'Level B (Warm/Considering)',
      'C': 'Level C (Cold/Inquiring)',
    };

    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({
        score: result.score,
        level: levelMap[result.score] || levelMap['C'],
        reasoning: result.reasoning,
      }),
      {
        status: 200,
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
          'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
        },
      }
    );
  } catch (err: any) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: err.message || 'Internal error' }),
      { status: 500, headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' } }
    );
  }
});

```

Scoring criteria:
- A (Hot/Ready): Clear budget, urgent timeline, high-quality source, specific project interest, ready to view/buy
- B (Warm/Considering): Moderate budget range, some urgency, considering options, needs follow-up
- C (Cold/Inquiring): Vague budget, no urgency, just browsing, low-quality source

      if (!res.ok) throw new Error('AI service unavailable');
      const reader = res.body?.getReader();
      const decoder = new TextDecoder();
      let fullText = '';
      if (reader) {
        while (true) {
          const { done, value } = await reader.read();
          if (done) break;
          const chunk = decoder.decode(value, { stream: true });
          for (const line of chunk.split('\n')) {
            const trimmed = line.trim();
            if (!trimmed.startsWith('data:')) continue;
            const dataStr = trimmed.slice(5).trim();
            if (!dataStr || dataStr === '[DONE]') continue;
            try {
              const parsed = JSON.parse(dataStr);
              const text = parsed.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text;
              if (text) fullText += text;
            } catch {
              // skip
            }
          }
        }
      }
      const jsonMatch = fullText.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/);
      if (!jsonMatch) throw new Error('Could not parse AI response');
      const result = JSON.parse(jsonMatch[0]);
      const score = String(result.score || 'C').trim().toUpperCase();
      const reasoning = String(result.reasoning || '');
      const levelMap: Record<string, string> = {
        'A': 'Level A (Hot/Ready)',
        'B': 'Level B (Warm/Considering)',
        'C': 'Level C (Cold/Inquiring)',
      };
      setLeadLevel(levelMap[score] || levelMap['C']);
      setAiScoreReason(reasoning);
      toast.success(`AI Score: ${score} — ${reasoning}`);
    } catch (err: any) {
      toast.error('AI စကိုးလုပ်ရာတွင် အမှားဖြစ်သွားပါသည်: ' + (err.message || ''));

Scoring criteria:
- A (Hot/Ready): Clear budget, urgent timeline, high-quality source, specific project interest, ready to view/buy
- B (Warm/Considering): Moderate budget range, some urgency, considering options, needs follow-up

      if (!res.ok) throw new Error('AI service unavailable');

      const decoder = new TextDecoder();
      let fullText = '';
      if (reader) {
        while (true) {
          const { done, value } = await reader.read();
          if (done) break;
          const chunk = decoder.decode(value, { stream: true });
          for (const line of chunk.split('\n')) {
            const trimmed = line.trim();
            if (!trimmed.startsWith('data:')) continue;
            const dataStr = trimmed.slice(5).trim();
            if (!dataStr || dataStr === '[DONE]') continue;
            try {
              const parsed = JSON.parse(dataStr);
              const text = parsed.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text;
              if (text) fullText += text;
            } catch {
              // skip
            }
          }
        }
      }
      const jsonMatch = fullText.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/);
      if (!jsonMatch) throw new Error('Could not parse AI response');
      const result = JSON.parse(jsonMatch[0]);
      const score = String(result.score || 'C').trim().toUpperCase();
      const reasoning = String(result.reasoning || '');
      const levelMap: Record<string, string> = {
        'A': 'Level A (Hot/Ready)',
        'B': 'Level B (Warm/Considering)',
        'C': 'Level C (Cold/Inquiring)',
      };
      const newLevel = levelMap[score] || levelMap['C'];
      // Update Firestore
      const { updateDoc, doc } = await import('firebase/firestore');
      const { db } = await import('@/lib/firebase');
      await updateDoc(doc(db, 'leads', lead.id), { leadLevel: newLevel });
      setLead((prev) => (prev ? { ...prev, leadLevel: newLevel } : prev));
      setAiScoreReason(reasoning);
      toast.success(`AI Re-score: ${score} — ${reasoning}`);

    30 function triggerDownload(blob: Blob, filename: string) {
    31   const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    32   const link = document.createElement('a');
    33   link.href = url;
    34   link.download = filename;
    35   link.style.display = 'none';
    36   document.body.appendChild(link);
    37   link.click();
    38   setTimeout(() => {
    39     document.body.removeChild(link);
    40     URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    41   }, 200);
    42 }

    44 export function exportAsExcel(leads: Lead[]) {

    46   const data = leads.map((l) => ({

   112     },
   113   });
   114 
   115   const blob = doc.output('blob');
   116   triggerDownload(blob, 'PSM_Leads_Report.pdf');

   119 export function exportAsCSV(leads: Lead[]) {
   120   if (leads.length === 0) return;
   121   const headers = ['Name', 'Phone', 'Project', 'Status'];
   122   const rows = leads.map((l) => [
   123     l.name,
   124     l.phone,
   125     l.preferredProject || '',
   126     l.status,
   127   ]);
   128   const csvContent = [headers, ...rows]
   129     .map((row) =>
   130       row.map((cell) => {
   131         const val = String(cell ?? '');
   132         if (val.includes(',') || val.includes('"') || val.includes('\n')) {
   133           return `"${val.replace(/"/g, '""')}"`;
   134         }
   135         return val;
   136       }).join(',')
   137     )
   138     .join('\n');
   139   const blob = new Blob(['\uFEFF' + csvContent], { type: 'text/csv;charset=utf-8;' });
   140   triggerDownload(blob, `PSM_Leads_${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.csv`);
   141 }
   142

   201 // ── KPI Export ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

   203 export function exportKPIAsExcel(
   204   agentStats: { email: string; totalLeads: number; totalCheckins: number; levelACount: number; levelBCount: number; levelCCount: number }[],
   205   departmentStats?: { displayName: string; totalLeads: number; levelACount: number; checkinCount: number; agentCount: number }[]
   206 ) {
   207   if (agentStats.length === 0) return;
   208 
   209   const wb = XLSX.utils.book_new();
   210 
   211   // Agent stats sheet
   212   const agentData = agentStats.map((a, idx) => ({
   213     'အဆင့်': idx + 1,
   214     'ဝန်ထမ်း': a.email,
   215     'စုစုပေါင်း Leads': a.totalLeads,
   216     'Check-ins': a.totalCheckins,
   217     'Level A': a.levelACount,
   218     'Level B': a.levelBCount,
   219     'Level C': a.levelCCount,
   220     'Conversion Rate': a.totalLeads > 0 ? `${((a.levelACount / a.totalLeads) * 100).toFixed(1)}%` : '0%',
   221   }));
   222   const agentWs = XLSX.utils.json_to_sheet(agentData);
   223   XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(wb, agentWs, 'ဝန်ထမ်း စွမ်းဆောင်ရည်');
   224 
   225   // Department stats sheet
   226   if (departmentStats && departmentStats.length > 0) {
   227     const deptData = departmentStats.map((d) => ({
   228       'ဌာန': d.displayName,
   229       'စုစုပေါင်း Leads': d.totalLeads,
   230       'Level A': d.levelACount,
   231       'Check-ins': d.checkinCount,
   232       'ဝန်ထမ်း အရေအတွက်': d.agentCount,
   233     }));
   234     const deptWs = XLSX.utils.json_to_sheet(deptData);
   235     XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(wb, deptWs, 'ဌာန စွမ်းဆောင်ရည်');
   236   }
   237 
   238   const buffer = XLSX.write(wb, { bookType: 'xlsx', type: 'array' });
   239   const blob = new Blob([buffer], { type: 'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet' });
   240   triggerDownload(blob, `PSM_KPI_Report_${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.xlsx`);
   241 }

   243 export function exportKPIAsPDF(
   244   agentStats: { email: string; totalLeads: number; totalCheckins: number; levelACount: number; levelBCount: number; levelCCount: number }[],
   245   departmentStats?: { displayName: string; totalLeads: number; levelACount: number; checkinCount: number; agentCount: number }[]
   246 ) {
   247   if (agentStats.length === 0) return;
   248   const doc = new jsPDF({ orientation: 'landscape', unit: 'mm', format: 'a4' });
   249 
   250   doc.setFontSize(16);
   251   doc.text('PSM Sale CRM - KPI Report', 14, 18);
   252   doc.setFontSize(10);
   253   doc.setTextColor(100);
   254   doc.text(`Generated on ${new Date().toLocaleDateString()}`, 14, 25);
   255 
   256   // Department summary
   257   let startY = 32;
   258   if (departmentStats && departmentStats.length > 0) {
   259     doc.setFontSize(12);
   260     doc.setTextColor(0);
   261     doc.text('Department Summary', 14, startY);
   262     startY += 4;
   263     autoTable(doc, {
   264       startY,
   265       head: [['ဌာန', 'Leads', 'Level A', 'Check-ins', 'ဝန်ထမ်းများ']],
   266       body: departmentStats.map((d) => [d.displayName, String(d.totalLeads), String(d.levelACount), String(d.checkinCount), String(d.agentCount)]),
   267       theme: 'striped',
   268       styles: { fontSize: 9, cellPadding: 2 },
   269       headStyles: { fillColor: [4, 99, 202], textColor: [255, 255, 255], fontStyle: 'bold' },
   270     });
   271     // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
   272     startY = (doc as any).lastAutoTable?.finalY + 10 || startY + 30;
   273   }
   274 
   275   // Agent performance
   276   doc.setFontSize(12);
   277   doc.setTextColor(0);
   278   doc.text('Agent Performance', 14, startY);
   279   autoTable(doc, {
   280     startY: startY + 4,
   281     head: [['#', 'ဝန်ထမ်း', 'Leads', 'Check-ins', 'Level A', 'Level B', 'Level C', 'Conversion']],
   282     body: agentStats.map((a, idx) => [
   283       String(idx + 1),
   284       a.email,
   285       String(a.totalLeads),
   286       String(a.totalCheckins),
   287       String(a.levelACount),
   288       String(a.levelBCount),
   289       String(a.levelCCount),
   290       a.totalLeads > 0 ? `${((a.levelACount / a.totalLeads) * 100).toFixed(1)}%` : '0%',
   291     ]),
   292     theme: 'striped',
   293     styles: { fontSize: 9, cellPadding: 2 },
   294     headStyles: { fillColor: [4, 99, 202], textColor: [255, 255, 255], fontStyle: 'bold' },
   295     alternateRowStyles: { fillColor: [248, 250, 252] },
   296   });
   297 
   298   const blob = doc.output('blob');
   299   triggerDownload(blob, `PSM_KPI_Report_${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.pdf`);
   300 }

```
// CSV Export Test — verifies exportAsCSV logic with sample lead data

interface TestLead {
  name: string;
  phone: string;
  preferredProject?: string;
  status: string;
}

function generateCSV(leads: TestLead[]): string {
  const headers = ['Name', 'Phone', 'Project', 'Status'];
  const rows = leads.map((l) => [
    l.name,
    l.phone,
    l.preferredProject || '',
    l.status,
  ]);
  return [headers, ...rows]
    .map((row) =>
      row.map((cell) => {
        const val = String(cell ?? '');
        if (val.includes(',') || val.includes('"') || val.includes('\n')) {
          return `"${val.replace(/"/g, '""')}"`;
        }
        return val;
      }).join(',')
    )
    .join('\n');
}

const sampleLeads: TestLead[] = [
  { name: 'Aung Kyaw', phone: '09951234567', preferredProject: 'Dagon Landmark Residence', status: 'New' },
  { name: 'Thida Win', phone: '09959876543', preferredProject: 'Emerald Bay Tower 3', status: 'Contacted' },
  { name: 'Myo Min, Dr.', phone: '09955678901', preferredProject: 'Perfect Signature Residence', status: 'Follow Up' },
  { name: 'Khin Lay', phone: '09953456789', preferredProject: 'Bahtoo Gyi Condo', status: 'Success' },
  { name: '"Special" Name', phone: '09951111111', status: 'New' },
];

const csvOutput = generateCSV(sampleLeads);

console.log('=== CSV Export Test Output ===\n');
console.log(csvOutput);
console.log('\n=== Validation ===');

const lines = csvOutput.split('\n');
console.log(`Header row: ${lines[0]}`);
console.log(`Expected header: Name,Phone,Project,Status`);
console.log(`Header match: ${lines[0] === 'Name,Phone,Project,Status' ? 'PASS ✓' : 'FAIL ✗'}`);

console.log(`\nTotal data rows: ${lines.length - 1} (expected: ${sampleLeads.length})`);
console.log(`Row count match: ${lines.length - 1 === sampleLeads.length ? 'PASS ✓' : 'FAIL ✗'}`);

// Verify comma escaping
const commaRow = lines.find((l) => l.includes('Myo Min'));
console.log(`\nComma in name escaped: ${commaRow?.startsWith('"') ? 'PASS ✓' : 'FAIL ✗'}`);
console.log(`Comma row: ${commaRow}`);

// Verify quote escaping
const quoteRow = lines.find((l) => l.includes('Special'));
console.log(`Quote in name escaped: ${quoteRow?.includes('""') ? 'PASS ✓' : 'FAIL ✗'}`);
console.log(`Quote row: ${quoteRow}`);

// Verify empty project handling
const emptyProjectRow = lines.find((l) => l.includes('09951111111'));
console.log(`Empty project handled: ${emptyProjectRow?.includes(',,') ? 'PASS ✓' : 'FAIL ✗'}`);
console.log(`Empty project row: ${emptyProjectRow}`);

console.log('\n=== All Tests Complete ===');

```

      setAiScoring(false);

  const handleAutoScore = async () => {
    const leadData = {
      name: name.trim(),
      phone: phone.trim(),
      email: email.trim() || undefined,
      interestType: interestType || undefined,
      propertyType: propertyType || undefined,
      preferredProject: preferredProject || undefined,
      budgetRange: budgetUnlimited ? 'Unlimited' : `MMK ${budgetMin.toLocaleString()} - ${budgetMax.toLocaleString()}`,
      purpose: purpose || undefined,
      urgency: urgency || undefined,
      paymentMethod: paymentMethod || undefined,
      leadSource: leadSource || undefined,
      currentLocation: currentLocation.trim() || undefined,
      remarks: remarks.trim() || undefined,
    };
    setAiScoring(true);
    setAiScoreReason('');
    try {
      const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('lead-score', {
        body: { lead: leadData },
      });
      if (error) {
        const errorMsg = await error?.context?.text();
        throw new Error(errorMsg || error.message || 'Edge function error');
      }
      if (!data || !data.score) throw new Error('Invalid response from AI');
      setLeadLevel(data.level || 'Level C (Cold/Inquiring)');
      setAiScoreReason(data.reasoning || '');
      toast.success(`AI Score: ${data.score} — ${data.reasoning}`);
    } catch (err: any) {
      toast.error('AI စကိုးလုပ်ရာတွင် အမှားဖြစ်သွားပါသည်: ' + (err.message || ''));
    } finally {
      setAiScoring(false);
    }
  };

     1 /**
     2  * Background Sync Client API
     3  *
     4  * Queues Firestore writes into an IndexedDB store when the device is offline.
     5  * When connectivity returns, the service worker fires a 'sync' event
     6  * which pulls items from the queue and asks the active client to perform
     7  * the actual Firestore write.
     8  */
     9 
    10 import { addDoc, collection, serverTimestamp } from 'firebase/firestore';
    11 import { db } from './firebase';
    12 import { isOnline, isNetworkError } from './offlineAuth';
    13 import { getFileQueueCount, flushStorageQueue } from './offlineStorageQueue';
    14 import { toast } from 'sonner';
    15 
    16 const DB_NAME = 'psm_offline_queue';
    17 const DB_VERSION = 2;
    18 
    19 interface QueueItem {
    20   id?: number;
    21   collection: string;
    22   payload: any;
    23   createdAt: number;
    24   retryCount: number;
    25 }
    26 
    27 function openQueueDb(): Promise<IDBDatabase> {
    28   return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    29     const req = indexedDB.open(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
    30     req.onupgradeneeded = () => {
    31       const database = req.result;
    32       if (!database.objectStoreNames.contains('checkins')) {
    33         database.createObjectStore('checkins', { keyPath: 'id', autoIncrement: true });
    34       }
    35       if (!database.objectStoreNames.contains('leads')) {
    36         database.createObjectStore('leads', { keyPath: 'id', autoIncrement: true });
    37       }
    38       if (!database.objectStoreNames.contains('audio_notes')) {
    39         database.createObjectStore('audio_notes', { keyPath: 'id', autoIncrement: true });
    40       }
    41       if (!database.objectStoreNames.contains('fileQueue')) {
    42         database.createObjectStore('fileQueue', { keyPath: 'id', autoIncrement: true });
    43       }
    44     };
    45     req.onsuccess = () => resolve(req.result);
    46     req.onerror = () => reject(req.error);
    47   });
    48 }
    49

   111 export async function submitCheckIn(payload: any): Promise<void> {
   112   try {
   113     await addDoc(collection(db, 'checkins'), {
   114       ...payload,
   115       timestamp: serverTimestamp(),
   116     });
   117   } catch (err: any) {
   118     if (isNetworkError(err) || !isOnline()) {
   119       await enqueue('checkins', payload);
   120       await requestSync('sync-checkin');
   121       toast.info('Check-in ကို offline queue တွင် သိမ်းဆည်းထားပါသည်။ အင်တာနက် ပြန်လာလျှင် auto-sync လုပ်ပေးပါမည်။');
   122       return;
   123     }
   124     throw err;
   125   }
   126 }
   127 
   128 /** Submit a lead. If offline, queue for background sync. */
   129 export async function submitLead(payload: any): Promise<void> {
   130   try {
   131     await addDoc(collection(db, 'leads'), {
   132       ...payload,
   133       createdAt: serverTimestamp(),
   134     });
   135   } catch (err: any) {
   136     if (isNetworkError(err) || !isOnline()) {
   137       await enqueue('leads', payload);

   183 export async function uploadFileWithFallback(
   184   fileType: FileType,
   185   storeName: string,
   186   payload: Record<string, any>,
   187   urlField: string,
   188   fileName: string,
   189   blob: Blob,
   190 ): Promise<string> {
   191   // Try online upload first
   192   try {
   193     const storageRef = ref(storage, fileName);
   194     const uploadResult = await uploadBytes(storageRef, blob);
   195     const downloadURL = await getDownloadURL(uploadResult.ref);
   196     return downloadURL;
   197   } catch (err: any) {
   198     // If network error, queue for later
   199     if (!isOnline() || err?.message?.toLowerCase().includes('network') || err?.code?.includes('network')) {
   200       await enqueueFileUpload(fileType, storeName, payload, urlField, fileName, blob);
   201       throw new Error('OFFLINE_QUEUED');
   202     }
   203     throw err;
   204   }
   205 }
   206

import React, { createContext, useContext, useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import type { Lang } from '@/lib/translations';
import { t as translate } from '@/lib/translations';

interface TranslationContextType {
  lang: Lang;
  setLang: (lang: Lang) => void;
  t: (key: string) => string;
}

const TranslationContext = createContext<TranslationContextType>({
  lang: 'mm',
  setLang: () => {},
  t: (key: string) => key,
});

export function TranslationProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const [lang, setLangState] = useState<Lang>(() => {
    const saved = localStorage.getItem('crm-lang') as Lang;
    return saved === 'en' ? 'en' : 'mm';
  });

  const setLang = useCallback((newLang: Lang) => {
    setLangState(newLang);
    localStorage.setItem('crm-lang', newLang);
  }, []);

  const t = useCallback(
    (key: string) => translate(key, lang),
    [lang]

--BEGIN AGENT OBSERVATION--
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import IntersectObserver from '@/components/common/IntersectObserver';
import SplashScreen from '@/components/common/SplashScreen';
import PWAInstallPrompt from '@/components/PWAInstallPrompt';
import { Toaster } from '@/components/ui/sonner';
import { AuthProvider } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
import { NotificationsProvider } from '@/contexts/NotificationsContext';
import { TranslationProvider } from '@/contexts/TranslationContext';
import { RouteGuard } from '@/components/common/RouteGuard';
import AppLayout from '@/components/layouts/AppLayout';

import { routes } from './routes';

const App: React.FC = () => {
  const [splashDone, setSplashDone] = useState(false);

  if (!splashDone) {
    return <SplashScreen onFinish={() => setSplashDone(true)} />;
  }

  return (
    <Router>
      <AuthProvider>
        <TranslationProvider>
        <NotificationsProvider>
        <RouteGuard>
          <IntersectObserver />
          <PWAInstallPrompt />
          <Routes>
            {routes
              .filter((r) => r.public)
              .map((route, index) => (
                <Route key={index} path={route.path} element={route.element} />
              ))}
            <Route
              path="/*"
              element={
                <AppLayout>
                  <Routes>
                    {routes
                      .filter((r) => !r.public)
                      .map((route, index) => (
                        <Route key={index} path={route.path} element={route.element} />
                      ))}
                    <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />} />
                    <Route path="/" element={<Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />} />
                  </Routes>
                </AppLayout>
              }
            />
          </Routes>
          <Toaster />
        </RouteGuard>
        </NotificationsProvider>
        </TranslationProvider>
      </AuthProvider>
    </Router>
  );
};

export default App;

function formatTimeAgo(ts: number): string {
  const diff = Date.now() - ts;
  const minutes = Math.floor(diff / 60000);
  if (minutes < 1) return 'ယခုပဲ';
  if (minutes < 60) return `${minutes} မိနစ်အကြာက`;
  const hours = Math.floor(minutes / 60);
  if (hours < 24) return `${hours} နာရီအကြာက`;
  return `${Math.floor(hours / 24)} ရက်အကြာက`;

import { serve } from 'https://deno.land/std@0.192.0/http/server.ts';

const API_ENDPOINT = 'https://app-chfyozakqsqp-api-VaOwP8E7dJqa.gateway.appmedo.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash:streamGenerateContent?alt=sse';

interface LeadData {
  name?: string;
  phone?: string;
  email?: string;
  interestType?: string;
  propertyType?: string;
  preferredProject?: string;
  budgetRange?: string;
  purpose?: string;
  urgency?: string;
  paymentMethod?: string;
  leadSource?: string;
  currentLocation?: string;
  remarks?: string;
}

function buildPrompt(lead: LeadData): string {
  return `You are a real estate CRM AI scoring assistant. Analyze the following lead data and score it as A, B, or C based on buying intent, budget clarity, urgency, and source quality.

Scoring criteria:
- A (Hot/Ready): Clear budget, urgent timeline, high-quality source, specific project interest, ready to view/buy
- B (Warm/Considering): Moderate budget range, some urgency, considering options, needs follow-up
- C (Cold/Inquiring): Vague budget, no urgency, just browsing, low-quality source

Lead data:
${JSON.stringify(lead, null, 2)}

Respond ONLY in this exact JSON format (no markdown, no extra text):
{"score":"A|B|C","reasoning":"brief reason in Myanmar language"}`;
}

async function callGemini(prompt: string, apiKey: string): Promise<{ score: string; reasoning: string }> {
  const body = {
    contents: [
      {
        role: 'user',
        parts: [{ text: prompt }],
      },
    ],
  };

  const response = await fetch(API_ENDPOINT, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      'X-Gateway-Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
    },
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
  });

  if (!response.ok) {
    const text = await response.text().catch(() => '');
    throw new Error(`Gemini API error ${response.status}: ${text}`);
  }

  const reader = response.body?.getReader();
  if (!reader) throw new Error('No response body');

  const decoder = new TextDecoder();
  let fullText = '';

  while (true) {
    const { done, value } = await reader.read();
    if (done) break;
    const chunk = decoder.decode(value, { stream: true });
    for (const line of chunk.split('\n')) {
      const trimmed = line.trim();
      if (!trimmed.startsWith('data:')) continue;
      const dataStr = trimmed.slice(5).trim();
      if (!dataStr || dataStr === '[DONE]') continue;
      try {
        const parsed = JSON.parse(dataStr);
        const text = parsed.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text;
        if (text) fullText += text;
      } catch {
        // skip malformed lines
      }
    }
  }

  // Extract JSON from response
  const jsonMatch = fullText.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/);
  if (!jsonMatch) {
    throw new Error('Could not parse AI response: ' + fullText.slice(0, 200));
  }

  const result = JSON.parse(jsonMatch[0]);
  return {
    score: String(result.score || 'C').trim().toUpperCase(),
    reasoning: String(result.reasoning || 'No reasoning provided.'),
  };
}

serve(async (req) => {
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') {
    return new Response(null, {
      status: 204,
      headers: {
        'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'POST, OPTIONS',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type, Authorization',
      },
    });
  }

  try {
    const apiKey = Deno.env.get('INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY');
    if (!apiKey) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ error: 'Server configuration error' }),
        { status: 500, headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' } }
      );
    }

    const { lead } = await req.json();
    if (!lead) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ error: 'Missing lead data' }),
        { status: 400, headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' } }
      );
    }

    const prompt = buildPrompt(lead);
    const result = await callGemini(prompt, apiKey);

    // Map to full level string
    const levelMap: Record<string, string> = {
      'A': 'Level A (Hot/Ready)',
      'B': 'Level B (Warm/Considering)',
      'C': 'Level C (Cold/Inquiring)',
    };

    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({
        score: result.score,
        level: levelMap[result.score] || levelMap['C'],
        reasoning: result.reasoning,
      }),
      {
        status: 200,
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
          'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
        },
      }
    );
  } catch (err: any) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: err.message || 'Internal error' }),
      { status: 500, headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' } }
    );
  }
});
[The command completed with exit code 0.]
